<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Popover.Description</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Popover.CloseTrigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Popover.Content</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Popover.Positioner</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Popover.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">open</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onOpenChange</code> props to control the open state of the popover.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the popover is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">usePopover</code> hook. This way you
can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="arrow" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#arrow"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Arrow</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Popover.Arrow</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Popover.ArrowTip</code> to render an arrow pointing to the trigger.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="placement" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#placement"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Placement</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To change the placement of the popover, set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">positioning</code> prop.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="close-behavior" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#close-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Close Behavior</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The popover is designed to close on blur and when the <kbd>esc</kbd> key is pressed.</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">To prevent it from closing on blur (clicking or focusing outside), pass the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">closeOnInteractOutside</code> prop and set it
to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">false</code>.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">To prevent it from closing when the <kbd>esc</kbd> key is pressed, pass the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">closeOnEsc</code> prop and set it to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">false</code>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="modality" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#modality"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Modality</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">In some cases, you might want the popover to be modal. This means that it&#x27;ll:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">trap focus within its content</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">block scrolling on the body</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">disable pointer interactions outside the popover</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">hide content behind the popover from screen readers</li>
</ul>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To make the popover modal, set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">modal</code> prop to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">true</code>. When <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">modal={true}</code>, we set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">portalled</code> attribute to
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">true</code> as well.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="anchor" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#anchor"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Anchor</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Popover.Anchor</code> to position the popover relative to a different element than the trigger.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9rhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9rhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9rhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="same-width" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#same-width"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Same Width</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">positioning.sameWidth</code> to make the popover match the width of its trigger element.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_a1hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_a1hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_a1hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="dialog-integration" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#dialog-integration"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Dialog Integration</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">When rendering a popover inside a dialog, you have two options for proper layering:</p>
<ol class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Keep the Portal with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">lazyMount</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">unmountOnExit</code></strong> - This ensures the popover is properly unmounted when the
dialog closes, preventing stale DOM nodes.</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Remove the Portal</strong> - Render the popover inline within the dialog content. This works well but may have z-index
considerations.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_a9hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_a9hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_a9hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="nested" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#nested"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Nested</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Popovers can be nested within each other. Each nested popover maintains its own open state and positioning.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_afhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_afhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_afhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="available-size" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#available-size"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Available Size</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The following css variables are exposed to the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Popover.Positioner</code> which you can use to style the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Popover.Content</code></p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">/* width of the popover trigger */</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">--reference-width: &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">pixel-value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">/* width of the available viewport */</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">--available-width: &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">pixel-value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">/* height of the available viewport */</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">--available-height: &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">pixel-value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span></code></pre>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">For example, if you want to make sure the maximum height doesn&#x27;t exceed the available height, use the following css:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-scope</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;popover&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">][</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-part</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;content&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  max-height</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">calc</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">var</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">--available-height</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">-</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> 100</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">px</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">Root</h3><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Prop</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Default</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Type</th></tr></thead><tbody class="table__body table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">autoFocus</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">true</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">boolean</code><p class="text">Whether to automatically set focus on the first focusable
content within the popover when opened.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm pressed.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code popover.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the open state of the popover.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">id</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-minus icon icon--size_xs c_fg.muted" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M5 12h14"></path></svg></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">string</code><p class="text">The unique identifier of the machine.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">ids</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-minus icon icon--size_xs c_fg.muted" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M5 12h14"></path></svg></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">Partial&lt;{

Useful for composition.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">immediate</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-minus icon icon--size_xs c_fg.muted" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M5 12h14"></path></svg></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">boolean</code><p class="text">Whether to synchronize the present change immediately or defer it to the next frame</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">initialFocusEl</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-minus icon icon--size_xs c_fg.muted" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M5 12h14"></path></svg></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">() =&gt; HTMLElement | null</code><p class="text">The element to focus on when the popover is opened.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">lazyMount</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">false</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">boolean</code><p class="text">Whether to enable lazy mounting</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">modal</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">false</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">boolean</code><p class="text">Whether the popover should be modal. When set to `true`:
- interaction with outside elements will be disabled
- only popover content will be visible to screen readers
- scrolling is blocked
- focus is trapped within the popover</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">onEscapeKeyDown</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-minus icon icon--size_xs c_fg.muted" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M5 12h14"></path></svg></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">(event: KeyboardEvent) =&gt; <div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPopover.Root\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eClick \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eFavorite Frameworks\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n            Manage and organize your favorite web frameworks.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/vue/popover'\nimport { Teleport } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPopover.Root\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner :class=\"styles.Positioner\"\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003eFavorite Frameworks\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e\n            Manage and organize your favorite web frameworks.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Popover } from '@ark-ui/svelte/popover'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPopover.Root\u003e\n  \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eFavorite Frameworks\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n          Manage and organize your favorite web frameworks.\n        \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled\n\nUse the `open` and `onOpenChange` props to control the open state of the popover.\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/react/popover'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false)\n  return (\n    \u003cPopover.Root open={open} onOpenChange={(e) =\u003e setOpen(e.open)}\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n            \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cPopover.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eTeam Members\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n            \u003cPopover.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n              Invite colleagues to collaborate on this project.\n            \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/solid/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [open, setOpen] = createSignal(false)\n  return (\n    \u003cPopover.Root open={open()} onOpenChange={(e) =\u003e setOpen(e.open)}\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n            \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eTeam Members\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n            \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n              Invite colleagues to collaborate on this project.\n            \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/vue/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref, Teleport } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nconst open = ref(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPopover.Root v-model:open=\"open\"\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner :class=\"styles.Positioner\"\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003eTeam Members\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e\n            Invite colleagues to collaborate on this project.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Popover } from '@ark-ui/svelte/popover'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { XIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\n  let open = $state(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPopover.Root bind:open\u003e\n  \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eTeam Members\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n          Invite colleagues to collaborate on this project.\n        \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the popover is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `usePopover` hook. This way you\ncan access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover, usePopover } from '@ark-ui/react/popover'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const popover = usePopover({\n    positioning: {\n      placement: 'bottom-start',\n    },\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cdiv\u003ePopover is {popover.open ? 'open' : 'closed'}\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.RootProvider value={popover}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eToggle Popover\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n            \u003cPopover.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n              \u003cPopover.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eControlled Externally\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n              \u003cPopover.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n                This popover is controlled via the usePopover hook.\n              \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n            \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover, usePopover } from '@ark-ui/solid/popover'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const popover = usePopover()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cdiv\u003ePopover is {popover().open ? 'open' : 'closed'}\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.RootProvider value={popover}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eToggle Popover\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n            \u003cPopover.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n              \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eControlled Externally\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n              \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n                This popover is controlled via the usePopover hook.\n              \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n            \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Popover, usePopover } from '@ark-ui/vue/popover'\nimport { Teleport } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nconst popover = usePopover({\n  positioning: {\n    placement: 'bottom-start',\n  },\n})\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv\u003ePopover is {{ popover.open ? 'open' : 'closed' }}\u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cPopover.RootProvider :value=\"popover\"\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Trigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eToggle Popover\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Positioner :class=\"styles.Positioner\"\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n            \u003cPopover.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003eControlled Externally\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n            \u003cPopover.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e\n              This popover is controlled via the usePopover hook.\n            \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n    \u003c/Popover.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Popover, usePopover } from '@ark-ui/svelte/popover'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\n  const popover = usePopover({\n    positioning: {\n      placement: 'bottom-start',\n    },\n  })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003cdiv\u003ePopover is {popover().open ? 'open' : 'closed'}\u003c/div\u003e\n\n  \u003cPopover.RootProvider value={popover}\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eToggle Popover\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eControlled Externally\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n            This popover is controlled via the usePopover hook.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Arrow\n\nUse `Popover.Arrow` and `Popover.ArrowTip` to render an arrow pointing to the trigger.\n\n**Example: arrow**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/react/popover'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const Arrow = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPopover.Root\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Arrow className={styles.Arrow}\u003e\n            \u003cPopover.ArrowTip className={styles.ArrowTip} /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.Arrow\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eNotifications\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n            You have 3 unread messages in your inbox.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/solid/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button  \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/vue/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { Teleport } from 'vue'\nimport button from have 3 unread messages in your inbox.\u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Placement\n\nTo change the placement of the popover, set the `positioning` prop.\n\n**Example: positioning**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/react/popover'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const Positioning = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPopover.Root\n    positioning={{\n      placement: 'left-start',\n      offset: { mainAxis: 12, crossAxis: 12 },\n    }}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eLeft Placement\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n            This popover appears on the left with custom offset values.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/solid/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const Positioning = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPopover.Root\n    positioning={{\n      placement: 'left-start',\n      offset: { mainAxis: 12, crossAxis: 12 },\n    }}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eLeft Placement\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n            This popover appears on the left with custom offset values.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/vue/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { Teleport } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPopover.Root\n    :positioning=\"{\n      placement: 'left-start',\n      offset: { mainAxis: 12, crossAxis: 12 },\n    }\"\n  \u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner :class=\"styles.Positioner\"\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003eLeft Placement\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e\n            This popover appears on the left with custom offset values.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Popover } from '@ark-ui/svelte/popover'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { XIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPopover.Root\n  positioning={{\n    placement: 'left-start',\n    offset: { mainAxis: 12, crossAxis: 12 },\n  }}\n\u003e\n  \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eLeft Placement\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n          This popover appears on the left with custom offset values.\n        \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Close Behavior\n\nThe popover is designed to close on blur and when the \u003ckbd\u003eesc\u003c/kbd\u003e key is pressed.\n\n- To prevent it from closing on blur (clicking or focusing outside), pass the `closeOnInteractOutside` prop and set it\n  to `false`.\n- To prevent it from closing when the \u003ckbd\u003eesc\u003c/kbd\u003e key is pressed, pass the `closeOnEsc` prop and set it to `false`.\n\n**Example: close-behavior**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/react/popover'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const CloseBehavior = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPopover.Root closeOnEscape closeOnInteractOutside\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eQuick Actions\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n            Press Escape or click outside to close this popover.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/solid/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const CloseBehavior = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPopover.Root closeOnEscape closeOnInteractOutside\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eQuick Actions\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n            Press Escape or click outside to close this popover.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/vue/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { Teleport } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPopover.Root closeOnEscape closeOnInteractOutside\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner :class=\"styles.Positioner\"\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003eQuick Actions\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e\n            Press Escape or click outside to close this popover.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Popover } from '@ark-ui/svelte/popover'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { XIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPopover.Root closeOnEscape closeOnInteractOutside\u003e\n  \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eQuick Actions\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n          Press Escape or click outside to close this popover.\n        \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Modality\n\nIn some cases, you might want the popover to be modal. This means that it'll:\n\n- trap focus within its content\n- block scrolling on the body\n- disable pointer interactions outside the popover\n- hide content behind the popover from screen readers\n\nTo make the popover modal, set the `modal` prop to `true`. When `modal={true}`, we set the `portalled` attribute to\n`true` as well.\n\n**Example: modal**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/react/popover'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const Modal = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPopover.Root modal\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eConfirm Action\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n            Focus is trapped inside this modal popover until dismissed.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/solid/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const Modal = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPopover.Root modal\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eConfirm Action\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n            Focus is trapped inside this modal popover until dismissed.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/vue/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { Teleport } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPopover.Root modal\u003e\n    \u003cPopover.Trigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner :class=\"styles.Positioner\"\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003eConfirm Action\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e\n            Focus is trapped inside this modal popover until dismissed.\n          \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Popover } from '@ark-ui/svelte/popover'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { XIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPopover.Root modal\u003e\n  \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eConfirm Action\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n          Focus is trapped inside this modal popover until dismissed.\n        \u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Anchor\n\nUse `Popover.Anchor` to position the popover relative to a different element than the trigger.\n\n**Example: anchor**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/react/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const Anchor = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cPopover.Root\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className=\"hstack\"\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Anchor className={styles.Anchor}\u003e\n          \u003cinput className={field.Input} placeholder=\"Type here...\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Anchor\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cPopover.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eTitle\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n          \u003cPopover.Description className={styles.Description}\u003eDescription\u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/solid/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/popover.module.css'\n\nexport const Anchor = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPopover.Root\u003e\n    \u003cdiv class=\"hstack\"\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eClick Me\u003c/Popover.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Anchor class={styles.Anchor}\u003e\n        \u003cinput class={field.Input} placeholder=\"Type here...\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Anchor\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cPopover.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n      \u003cPopover.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Popover.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eTitle\u003c/Popover.Title\u003e\n        \u003cPopover.Description class={styles.Description}\u003eDescription\u003c/Popover.Description\u003e\n      \u003c/Popover.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Popover.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Popover.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Popover } from '@ark-ui/vue/popover'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from
